## פאה (id: 005773000000000)

פאה
===

פאה (H6284)

verb · פֵּאָה

Non\-Exist

to destroy, to wipe out, to strike down exact meaning unsure; probably: \= causative action by which humans take the life of other humans in a violent way

[DEU 32:26](https://ref.ly/Deut32:26)1

1 DEU 32:26 NJB NJPS REB GNT \| RSV NIV NRSV CEV אֲפִיצֵם \= פוץ "to scatter"

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Deuteronomy 32:26

Objects

frontier land literally: side (of land); hence: \= area of land located on the boundary of one's territory; ► functions as buffer between one's own territory and that of the neighboring countries

[NEH 9:22](https://ref.ly/Neh9:22)

People

temple literally: side (of head); hence: \= side of the head between forehead and ear; ► the hair of which was not be shaved as was the practice of certain ethnic groups

[NUM 24:17](https://ref.ly/Num24:17) · [JER 9:25](https://ref.ly/Jer9:25) · [JER 25:23](https://ref.ly/Jer25:23) · [JER 48:45](https://ref.ly/Jer48:45) · [JER 49:32](https://ref.ly/Jer49:32)

noun f · יפה

Good

beauty, quality, luxury \= high quality of beauty

[AMO 3:12](https://ref.ly/Amos3:12)2

1 AMO 3:12 RSV NIV NJB NJPS NRSV CEV \[1] \| REB GNT \[2] 2 AMO 3:12 \| REB GNT \[2] \| RSV NIV NJB NJPS NRSV CEV \[1]

Reinier de Blois

## פאר (id: 005775000000000)

פאר
===

פאר (H6286)

verb · פְּאֵר · פֹּארָה · פֻּארָה · פָּארוּר

See

to check the branches \= action by which humans check the branches of a tree after having beaten it; ► in order to find any remaining fruit

[DEU 24:20](https://ref.ly/Deut24:20)

verb · תִּפְאָרָה · תִּפְאֶרֶת

Great

to receive honor, to receive praise \= state in which humans or deities are considered worthy of honor and respect more than others

[EXO 8:5](https://ref.ly/Exod8:5) · [ISA 44:23](https://ref.ly/Isa44:23) · [ISA 49:3](https://ref.ly/Isa49:3) · [ISA 60:21](https://ref.ly/Isa60:21) · [ISA 61:3](https://ref.ly/Isa61:3)

Great

to vaunt oneself over, to claim to be greater than (someone else) \= state in which humans consider themselves more worthy of honor and respect than others and act accordingly

[JDG 7:2](https://ref.ly/Judg7:2) · [ISA 10:15](https://ref.ly/Isa10:15)

Great

to honor, to make glorious, to make great \= causative action by which deities cause humans or objects to have honor, majesty and splendor

[EZR 7:27](https://ref.ly/Ezra7:27) · [PSA 149:4](https://ref.ly/Ps149:4) · [ISA 55:5](https://ref.ly/Isa55:5) · [ISA 60:7](https://ref.ly/Isa60:7) · [ISA 60:9](https://ref.ly/Isa60:9) · [ISA 60:13](https://ref.ly/Isa60:13)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Deuteronomy 24:20; Exodus 8:5; Isaiah 44:23; Isaiah 49:3; Isaiah 60:21; Isaiah 61:3; Judges 7:2; Isaiah 10:15; Ezra 7:27; Psalms 149:4; Isaiah 55:5; Isaiah 60:7; Isaiah 60:9; Isaiah 60:13


## פְּאֵר (id: 005776000000000)

פְּאֵר
======

פְּאֵר (H6287)

noun m · פאר

Clothing

turban \= head\-dress; ◄ made out of cloth; ► worn by priests, but also by ordinary men and women, probably on special occasions; not to be worn when in mourning; ≈ therefore associated with joy

[ISA 3:20](https://ref.ly/Isa3:20) · [ISA 61:3](https://ref.ly/Isa61:3) · [EZK 24:17](https://ref.ly/Ezek24:17) · [EZK 24:23](https://ref.ly/Ezek24:23) · [ISA 61:10](https://ref.ly/Isa61:10) · [EZK 44:18](https://ref.ly/Ezek44:18) · [EXO 39:28](https://ref.ly/Exod39:28)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Isaiah 3:20; Isaiah 61:3; Ezekiel 24:17; Ezekiel 24:23; Isaiah 61:10; Ezekiel 44:18; Exodus 39:28

## פגע (id: 005783000000000)

פגע
===

פגע (H6293)

verb · פֶּגַע · מִפְגָּע

Meet

to meet, to run into, to find, to come across, to come upon \= process by which humans or animals unexpectedly meet other humans or animals while travelling from one location to another

[EXO 5:20](https://ref.ly/Exod5:20) · [EXO 23:4](https://ref.ly/Exod23:4) · [1SA 10:5](https://ref.ly/1Sam10:5) · [AMO 5:19](https://ref.ly/Amos5:19)

Meet

to meet, to reach, to find \= process by which humans meet other humans or reach an object while travelling from one location to another

[GEN 28:11](https://ref.ly/Gen28:11) · [GEN 32:2](https://ref.ly/Gen32:2) · [NUM 35:19](https://ref.ly/Num35:19) · [NUM 35:21](https://ref.ly/Num35:21) · [JOS 2:16](https://ref.ly/Josh2:16) · [JOS 16:7](https://ref.ly/Josh16:7) · [JOS 17:10](https://ref.ly/Josh17:10) · [JOS 19:11](https://ref.ly/Josh19:11) · [JOS 19:11](https://ref.ly/Josh19:11) · [JOS 19:22](https://ref.ly/Josh19:22) · [JOS 19:26](https://ref.ly/Josh19:26) · [JOS 19:27](https://ref.ly/Josh19:27) · [JOS 19:34](https://ref.ly/Josh19:34) · [JOS 19:34](https://ref.ly/Josh19:34) · [ISA 47:3](https://ref.ly/Isa47:3)2

Meet

to molest, to strike down, to punish \= action by which humans go and meet other humans ► with the purpose of killing or harming that person

[EXO 5:3](https://ref.ly/Exod5:3) · [JDG 8:21](https://ref.ly/Judg8:21) · [JDG 15:12](https://ref.ly/Judg15:12) · [JDG 18:25](https://ref.ly/Judg18:25) · [RUT 2:22](https://ref.ly/Ruth2:22) · [1SA 22:17](https://ref.ly/1Sam22:17) · [1SA 22:18](https://ref.ly/1Sam22:18) · [1SA 22:18](https://ref.ly/1Sam22:18) · [2SA 1:15](https://ref.ly/2Sam1:15) · [1KI 2:25](https://ref.ly/1Kgs2:25) · [1KI 2:29](https://ref.ly/1Kgs2:29) · [1KI 2:31](https://ref.ly/1Kgs2:31) · [1KI 2:32](https://ref.ly/1Kgs2:32) · [1KI 2:34](https://ref.ly/1Kgs2:34) · [1KI 2:46](https://ref.ly/1Kgs2:46) · [ISA 64:4](https://ref.ly/Isa64:4)1

Meet

to cause to reach \= causative action by which deities cause objects to go and reach another object

[JOB 36:32](https://ref.ly/Job36:32)

Bear

to cause (something) to meet (someone) \> to make (someone) responsible for (something) literally: to cause an event to meet someone; hence: \= causative action by which deities make humans responsible for an event

[ISA 53:6](https://ref.ly/Isa53:6)

Speak

to entreat, to beg, to intercede literally: to meet; hence: \= action by which humans address other humans with humility and politeness, ► with the purpose of asking for a favor

[GEN 23:8](https://ref.ly/Gen23:8) · [RUT 1:16](https://ref.ly/Ruth1:16) · [ISA 53:12](https://ref.ly/Isa53:12) · [JER 36:25](https://ref.ly/Jer36:25)

Pray

to entreat, to pray, to intercede \= action by which humans address deities with humility and politeness, ► with the purpose of asking for a favor

[JOB 21:15](https://ref.ly/Job21:15) · [ISA 47:3](https://ref.ly/Isa47:3)2 · [ISA 59:16](https://ref.ly/Isa59:16) · [JER 7:16](https://ref.ly/Jer7:16) · [JER 15:11](https://ref.ly/Jer15:11) · [JER 27:18](https://ref.ly/Jer27:18)

1 ISA 64:4 NJPS \| RSV NIV NJB NRSV REB GNT CEV "to meet, to welcome, to receive" 2 ISA 47:3 MT HOTTP\-C RSV NIV NRSV REB CEV \[b] \| NJPS \[f] \| NJB GNT יִפְגַּע

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Exodus 5:20; Exodus 23:4; 1 Samuel 10:5; Amos 5:19; Genesis 28:11; Genesis 32:2; Numbers 35:19; Numbers 35:21; Joshua 2:16; Joshua 16:7; Joshua 17:10; Joshua 19:11; Joshua 19:22; Joshua 19:26; Joshua 19:27; Joshua 19:34; Isaiah 47:3; Exodus 5:3; Judges 8:21; Judges 15:12; Judges 18:25; Ruth 2:22; 1 Samuel 22:17; 1 Samuel 22:18; 2 Samuel 1:15; 1 Kings 2:25; 1 Kings 2:29; 1 Kings 2:31; 1 Kings 2:32; 1 Kings 2:34; 1 Kings 2:46; Isaiah 64:4; Job 36:32; Isaiah 53:6; Genesis 23:8; Ruth 1:16; Isaiah 53:12; Jeremiah 36:25; Job 21:15; Isaiah 59:16; Jeremiah 7:16; Jeremiah 15:11; Jeremiah 27:18

## פגשׁ (id: 005788000000000)

פגשׁ
====

פגשׁ (H6298)

verb

Meet

to meet, to run into, to find, to come across, to come upon \= process by which humans, animals, or deities come upon other humans or animals while travelling from one location to another, either or not expectedly; these encounters may be peaceful or result in aggression depending on the nature or intentions of one or both parties

[GEN 32:18](https://ref.ly/Gen32:18) · [GEN 33:8](https://ref.ly/Gen33:8) · [EXO 4:24](https://ref.ly/Exod4:24) · [EXO 4:27](https://ref.ly/Exod4:27) · [1SA 25:20](https://ref.ly/1Sam25:20) · [2SA 2:13](https://ref.ly/2Sam2:13) · [PRO 17:12](https://ref.ly/Prov17:12) · [JER 41:6](https://ref.ly/Jer41:6) · [HOS 13:8](https://ref.ly/Hos13:8)

Space · Associate

to live alongside (someone else) literally: to meet; hence: \= process by which humans share a space with other humans where they have certain interests in common and may run into each other occasionally; ≈ used figuratively for animals only

[ISA 34:14](https://ref.ly/Isa34:14)

Space · Associate

to live alongside one another literally: to meet one another; hence: \= process by which humans share the same space where they have certain interests in common and may run into each other occasionally

[PSA 85:11](https://ref.ly/Ps85:11) · [PRO 22:2](https://ref.ly/Prov22:2) · [PRO 29:13](https://ref.ly/Prov29:13)

Happen

to encounter literally: to meet with an event; hence: \= process by which humans undergo an event ◄ as if it where another human they met with on the road

[JOB 5:14](https://ref.ly/Job5:14)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Genesis 32:18; Genesis 33:8; Exodus 4:24; Exodus 4:27; 1 Samuel 25:20; 2 Samuel 2:13; Proverbs 17:12; Jeremiah 41:6; Hosea 13:8; Isaiah 34:14; Psalms 85:11; Proverbs 22:2; Proverbs 29:13; Job 5:14


## פדה (id: 005789000000000)

פדה
===

פדה (H6299) [SAHD](https://sahd-online.com/words/p-d-h/)

verb · פְּדוּיִם · פְּדוּת · פִּדְיֹום · פִּדְיֹון · פְּדָהאֵל · פָּדֹון · פְּדָיָה · פְּדָיָהוּ · פְּדָהצוּר

Exchange

to ransom, to redeem \= causative action by which humans exchange animals or other humans by substituting them with money or with an(other) animal, ► as a result of which they will escape death or slavery

[EXO 13:13](https://ref.ly/Exod13:13) · [EXO 13:13](https://ref.ly/Exod13:13) · [EXO 13:13](https://ref.ly/Exod13:13) · [EXO 13:15](https://ref.ly/Exod13:15) · [EXO 34:20](https://ref.ly/Exod34:20) · [EXO 34:20](https://ref.ly/Exod34:20) · [EXO 34:20](https://ref.ly/Exod34:20) · [LEV 19:20](https://ref.ly/Lev19:20) · [LEV 19:20](https://ref.ly/Lev19:20) · [LEV 27:27](https://ref.ly/Lev27:27) · [LEV 27:29](https://ref.ly/Lev27:29) · [NUM 18:15](https://ref.ly/Num18:15) · [NUM 18:15](https://ref.ly/Num18:15) · [NUM 18:15](https://ref.ly/Num18:15) · [NUM 18:16](https://ref.ly/Num18:16) · [NUM 18:17](https://ref.ly/Num18:17) · [PSA 49:8](https://ref.ly/Ps49:8) · [PSA 49:8](https://ref.ly/Ps49:8)

Exchange

to have (someone) redeemed, to have (someone) ransomed \= causative action by which humans cause other humans to be exchanged by substituting them with money, ► as a result of which they will escape slavery

[EXO 21:8](https://ref.ly/Exod21:8)

Safe

to redeem, to save, to deliver literally: to redeem, ransom; hence: \= causative action by which humans or deities help (other) humans out of a dangerous, life\-threatening, or otherwise difficult situation

[DEU 7:8](https://ref.ly/Deut7:8) · [DEU 9:26](https://ref.ly/Deut9:26) · [DEU 13:6](https://ref.ly/Deut13:6) · [DEU 15:15](https://ref.ly/Deut15:15) · [DEU 21:8](https://ref.ly/Deut21:8) · [DEU 24:18](https://ref.ly/Deut24:18) · [1SA 14:45](https://ref.ly/1Sam14:45) · [2SA 4:9](https://ref.ly/2Sam4:9) · [2SA 7:23](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:23) · [2SA 7:23](https://ref.ly/2Sam7:23) · [1KI 1:29](https://ref.ly/1Kgs1:29) · [1CH 17:21](https://ref.ly/1Chr17:21) · [1CH 17:21](https://ref.ly/1Chr17:21) · [NEH 1:10](https://ref.ly/Neh1:10) · [JOB 5:20](https://ref.ly/Job5:20) · [JOB 6:23](https://ref.ly/Job6:23) · [JOB 33:28](https://ref.ly/Job33:28) · [PSA 25:22](https://ref.ly/Ps25:22) · [PSA 26:11](https://ref.ly/Ps26:11) · [PSA 31:6](https://ref.ly/Ps31:6) · [PSA 34:23](https://ref.ly/Ps34:23) · [PSA 44:27](https://ref.ly/Ps44:27) · [PSA 49:16](https://ref.ly/Ps49:16) · [PSA 55:19](https://ref.ly/Ps55:19) · [PSA 69:19](https://ref.ly/Ps69:19) · [PSA 71:23](https://ref.ly/Ps71:23) · [PSA 78:42](https://ref.ly/Ps78:42) · [PSA 119:134](https://ref.ly/Ps119:134) · [PSA 130:8](https://ref.ly/Ps130:8) · [ISA 1:27](https://ref.ly/Isa1:27) · [ISA 29:22](https://ref.ly/Isa29:22) · [ISA 35:10](https://ref.ly/Isa35:10) · [ISA 51:11](https://ref.ly/Isa51:11) · [JER 15:21](https://ref.ly/Jer15:21) · [JER 31:11](https://ref.ly/Jer31:11) · [HOS 7:13](https://ref.ly/Hos7:13) · [HOS 13:14](https://ref.ly/Hos13:14) · [MIC 6:4](https://ref.ly/Mic6:4) · [ZEC 10:8](https://ref.ly/Zech10:8)

## פוח (id: 005809000000000)

פוח
===

פוח (H6315)

verb · פִּיחַ

[SNG 4:16](https://ref.ly/Song4:16) · [EZK 21:36](https://ref.ly/Ezek21:36)

[PRO 29:8](https://ref.ly/Prov29:8)

Speak

to sneer literally: to blow (at people); hence: \= action by which humans express their anger towards other humans

[PSA 10:5](https://ref.ly/Ps10:5)

to utter literally: to blow; hence: \= action by which humans utter words, which can be either truthful or lying

## פוץ (id: 005821000000000)

פוץ
===

פוץ (H6327a · H6327b · H6327c · H6327d) — פּוּצַי

verb · מֵפִיץ · תְּפֹוצָה

Scatter

to be scattered, to be dispersed, to spread \= process by which humans or animals leave their normal location and move away in different directions, usually not of their own volition

[GEN 10:18](https://ref.ly/Gen10:18) · [GEN 11:4](https://ref.ly/Gen11:4) · [NUM 10:35](https://ref.ly/Num10:35) · [1SA 11:11](https://ref.ly/1Sam11:11) · [2SA 18:8](https://ref.ly/2Sam18:8) · [1KI 22:17](https://ref.ly/1Kgs22:17) · [2KI 25:5](https://ref.ly/2Kgs25:5) · [2CH 18:16](https://ref.ly/2Chr18:16) · [PSA 68:2](https://ref.ly/Ps68:2) · [ISA 11:12](https://ref.ly/Isa11:12) · [JER 10:21](https://ref.ly/Jer10:21) · [JER 40:15](https://ref.ly/Jer40:15) · [JER 52:8](https://ref.ly/Jer52:8) · [EZK 11:17](https://ref.ly/Ezek11:17) · [EZK 20:34](https://ref.ly/Ezek20:34) · [EZK 20:41](https://ref.ly/Ezek20:41) · [EZK 28:25](https://ref.ly/Ezek28:25) · [EZK 29:13](https://ref.ly/Ezek29:13) · [EZK 34:5](https://ref.ly/Ezek34:5) · [EZK 34:5](https://ref.ly/Ezek34:5) · [EZK 34:6](https://ref.ly/Ezek34:6) · [EZK 34:12](https://ref.ly/Ezek34:12) · [ZEP 3:10](https://ref.ly/Zeph3:10)2 · [ZEC 13:7](https://ref.ly/Zech13:7)

Scatter

to disperse \= action by which humans leave their location and move away in different directions

[EXO 5:12](https://ref.ly/Exod5:12) · [1SA 13:8](https://ref.ly/1Sam13:8) · [1SA 14:34](https://ref.ly/1Sam14:34) · [2SA 20:22](https://ref.ly/2Sam20:22)

Scatter

Safe

to carry off, to bring into security \= causative action by which animals remove objects from a situation regarded as threatening by them

[ISA 5:29](https://ref.ly/Isa5:29)

Birth

to deliver (as in childbirth), to bring forth, to calve literally: to deliver; hence: \= causative action by which human or animal females give birth to offspring

[JOB 21:10](https://ref.ly/Job21:10) · [MIC 6:14](https://ref.ly/Mic6:14)

Birth

to deliver, bring forth a child literally: to deliver; hence: \= causative action by which human females give birth to offspring, with focus on a successful completion of the process

[MIC 6:14](https://ref.ly/Mic6:14)

1 JOB 23:7 The piel is often revocalized as a qal. 2 PSA 56:8 NIV REB ESV \| RSV "recompense" NRSV "repay" GNT "punish" \= פלס \| NJPS "cast out" NJB "reject"

P.J. Williams

* **Associated Passages:** Job 23:7; Ezekiel 7:16; 2 Samuel 22:44; Psalms 17:13; Psalms 18:44; Psalms 18:49; Psalms 22:5; Psalms 22:9; Psalms 31:2; Psalms 32:7; Psalms 37:40; Psalms 43:1; Psalms 56:8; Psalms 71:2; Psalms 71:4; Psalms 82:4; Psalms 91:14; 2 Samuel 22:2; Psalms 18:3; Psalms 40:18; Psalms 70:6; Psalms 144:2; Isaiah 5:29; Job 21:10; Micah 6:14

Reinier de Blois

## פלס (id: 005909000000000)

פלס
===

פלס (H6424)

verb · פֶּלֶס

Angry

**Collocation:** פלס נָתִיב לְאַף

to give free course to (one's) anger literally: to make level a path for (one's) anger; hence: \= action by which deities give full vent to their anger

[PSA 78:50](https://ref.ly/Ps78:50)

Easy

to make easy literally: to make level (a road or path for someone else); hence: \= causative action by which deities allow humans to make their journey to life without major obstacles

[ISA 26:7](https://ref.ly/Isa26:7)

Happen

to deal out, to promote literally: to make level; hence: \= causative action by which humans in authority use their power or influence to promote a certain type of behavior

[PSA 58:3](https://ref.ly/Ps58:3)

Think

to consider carefully literally: to make level (a road or path); hence: \= action by which humans pay careful attention to the course of action ahead of them

[PRO 4:26](https://ref.ly/Prov4:26) · [PRO 5:6](https://ref.ly/Prov5:6)

Think

to consider carefully literally: to make level (a road or path); hence: \= action by which deities pay careful attention to the course of action taken by humans

[PRO 5:21](https://ref.ly/Prov5:21)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Psalms 78:50; Isaiah 26:7; Psalms 58:3; Proverbs 4:26; Proverbs 5:6; Proverbs 5:21


## פֶּלֶס (id: 005910000000000)

פֶּלֶס
======

פֶּלֶס (H6425)

noun m · פלס

Tools

balance, scales \= contraption consisting of rod held by a cord in the middle and with pans attached to both ends; ► used for weighing objects

[PRO 16:11](https://ref.ly/Prov16:11) · [ISA 40:12](https://ref.ly/Isa40:12)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Proverbs 16:11; Isaiah 40:12

## פַּלָּצוּת (id: 005912000000000)

פַּלָּצוּת
==========

פַּלָּצוּת (H6427)

noun f · פלץ

Unsteady · Afraid

trembling \= process by which the human body shakes, ◄ as a result of fear

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Job 21:6; Psalms 55:6; Isaiah 21:4; Ezekiel 7:18


## פלשׁ (id: 005913000000000)

פלשׁ
====

פלשׁ (H6428)

verb

Turn

to roll, to wallow \= action by which humans turn about in a substance, so that their body or clothing is covered by it

## פְּלֶשֶׁת (id: 005914000000000)

פְּלֶשֶׁת

פְּלֶשֶׁת (H6429)

name · פְּלִשְׁתִּי

Philistia \= land of the Philistines, situated along the coast of the Meditteranean and concentrated around the cities of Gaza, Gath, Ekron, Ashdod, and Ashkelon

פִּנָּה
=======

noun f

Constructions

**Collocation:** אֶבֶן לְפִנָּה · אֶבֶן פִּנָּה

cornerstone literally: stone of corner, stone for corner; hence: \= a stone that forms the base of a corner of a building or city wall, joining two walls; ≈ regarded as a very important stone within a construction as it gives crucial support to the entire structure

## פְּקֻדָּה (id: 005973000000000)

פְּקֻדָּה
=========

פְּקֻדָּה (H6486)

noun f · פקד

See

muster \= action by which humans carefully observe a relatively large group of people or objects, ► with the purpose of determining their number, establishing whether everyone is present, or, in the case of an army, to get to know their fighting strength

[2CH 17:14](https://ref.ly/2Chr17:14) · [2CH 26:11](https://ref.ly/2Chr26:11)

Know

notice, providence literally: muster; hence: \= action by which deities take notice of the misfortune or suffering of (other) humans and intervene in order to help

Chastise

punishment literally: notice; hence: \= action by which deities or humans inflict a penalty on other deities, humans, animals, or objects, usually as retribution for an offence

## פקח (id: 005978000000000)

פקח
===

פקח (H6491)

verb · פִּקֵּחַ · פְּקַח־קֹוחַ

Able

**Collocation:** פקח עֵינַיִם

to make see literally: to open (someone else's) eyes; hence: \= causative action by which deities give humans the ability to see things that they were not able to see before

[GEN 3:5](https://ref.ly/Gen3:5) · [GEN 3:7](https://ref.ly/Gen3:7) · [GEN 21:19](https://ref.ly/Gen21:19) · [2KI 6:17](https://ref.ly/2Kgs6:17) · [2KI 6:17](https://ref.ly/2Kgs6:17) · [2KI 6:20](https://ref.ly/2Kgs6:20) · [2KI 6:20](https://ref.ly/2Kgs6:20) · [PSA 146:8](https://ref.ly/Ps146:8) · [ISA 35:5](https://ref.ly/Isa35:5) · [ISA 42:7](https://ref.ly/Isa42:7)

**Collocation:** פקח עֵינַיִם

to wake up literally: to open (one's) eyes; hence: \= process by which humans wake up from sleep or death

[2KI 4:35](https://ref.ly/2Kgs4:35) · [JOB 27:19](https://ref.ly/Job27:19)

**Collocation:** פקח עֵינַיִם

## פַּקֻּעֹת (id: 005985000000000)

פַּקֻּעֹת
=========

פַּקֻּעֹת (H6498)

noun f · פְּקָעִים

Fruits

wild gourd \= a fruit that looks like a melon, cucumber, or calabash vine; it has a thick, watery root, which can penetrate deep into the ground; its stems creep on the ground, clinging to bushes or fences with their tendrils; its leaves are triangular and lobed like melon leaves; its yellow flowers develop into round yellow fruits the size of a large apple or grapefruit; the shell of the fruit is hard and smooth, and inside is a spongy pulp with white or brown seeds; ◄ Citrullus colocynthis; ► slightly poisonous, but used for stomach disorders and as a purgative

## פרה (id: 005995000000000)

פרה
===

פרה (H6500 · H6509) — פרא, פֹּרָת

verb · פְּרִי

Stage

to grow, to sprout \= process by which a branch grows out of the stump or the root of a tree, or by which a plant grows directly out of the soil

[ISA 11:1](https://ref.ly/Isa11:1) · [ISA 45:8](https://ref.ly/Isa45:8)

Stage

to bear, to cause to grow, to cause to sprout \= causative process by which a plant causes a branch to grow out of its roots

[DEU 29:17](https://ref.ly/Deut29:17)

Quantity

to be fruitful, to flourish, to increase literally: to sprout; hence; \= process by which humans, animals, or plants produce much offspring, ► and so grow in number and strength

[GEN 1:22](https://ref.ly/Gen1:22) · [GEN 1:28](https://ref.ly/Gen1:28) · [GEN 8:17](https://ref.ly/Gen8:17) · [GEN 9:1](https://ref.ly/Gen9:1) · [GEN 9:7](https://ref.ly/Gen9:7) · [GEN 26:22](https://ref.ly/Gen26:22) · [GEN 35:11](https://ref.ly/Gen35:11) · [GEN 47:27](https://ref.ly/Gen47:27) · [GEN 49:22](https://ref.ly/Gen49:22)1 · [GEN 49:22](https://ref.ly/Gen49:22)1 · [EXO 1:7](https://ref.ly/Exod1:7) · [EXO 23:30](https://ref.ly/Exod23:30) · [PSA 128:3](https://ref.ly/Ps128:3) · [ISA 17:6](https://ref.ly/Isa17:6) · [ISA 32:12](https://ref.ly/Isa32:12) · [JER 3:16](https://ref.ly/Jer3:16) · [JER 23:3](https://ref.ly/Jer23:3) · [EZK 19:10](https://ref.ly/Ezek19:10) · [EZK 36:11](https://ref.ly/Ezek36:11) · [HOS 13:15](https://ref.ly/Hos13:15)

Quantity

to make fruitful, to make flourish, to cause to increase literally: to cause to sprout; hence: \= causative action by which a deity causes humans to produce much offspring, ► and so grow in number and strength

[GEN 17:6](https://ref.ly/Gen17:6) · [GEN 17:20](https://ref.ly/Gen17:20) · [GEN 28:3](https://ref.ly/Gen28:3) · [GEN 41:52](https://ref.ly/Gen41:52) · [GEN 48:4](https://ref.ly/Gen48:4) · [LEV 26:9](https://ref.ly/Lev26:9) · [PSA 105:24](https://ref.ly/Ps105:24)

1 GEN 49:22 · GEN 49:22 MT בֵּן פֹּרָת \| RSV NRSV ESV "fruitful bough" NJB "fruitful plant" REB "fruitful tree" CEV "fruitful vine" \| NJPS "wild ass" GNT "wild donkey" \| LXX "υἱὸς ηὑξημέμος" (\= "grown son") VUL "filius adcrescens" (\= "son growing up")

Reinier de Blois

## פרח (id: 006008000000000)

פרח
===

פרח (H6524)

verb · אֶפְרֹחַ · פֶּרַח · פָּרוּחַ

Stage

to break out, to sprout, to bud, to blossom, to spread, to erupt, to flourish \= process by which living organisms mature and develop in their natural way, such as plants developing flowers, sicknesses spreading, etc.; ≈ often used figuratively to denote developments in human life and behavior

Stage

to make break forth, to make bud \= causative process by which deities and humans cause living organisms to mature and develop in their natural way, such as plants developing flowers

[ISA 17:11](https://ref.ly/Isa17:11) · [EZK 17:24](https://ref.ly/Ezek17:24)

Safe

to flourish literally: to flourish; hence: \= state in which people are experiencing prosperity in the place where they live, ◄ like a blossoming flower

verb

Birds

bird exact meaning unsure; probably, literally: those that fly; hence: \= a reference to a bird

===

פרע (H6544)

verb · פֶּרַע

Release

to let hang loose exact meaning unsure; probably: \= action by which humans bare their heads and allow their long hair to hang loose

[LEV 10:6](https://ref.ly/Lev10:6) · [LEV 13:45](https://ref.ly/Lev13:45) · [LEV 21:10](https://ref.ly/Lev21:10) · [NUM 5:18](https://ref.ly/Num5:18) · [JDG 5:2](https://ref.ly/Judg5:2)1

Free

to lose control literally: to break loose; hence: \= process by which a group of people runs out of control

[EXO 32:25](https://ref.ly/Exod32:25) · [PRO 29:18](https://ref.ly/Prov29:18)

Free

to cause to lose control literally: to cause to break loose; hence: \= causative process by which humans allow a group of people to run out of control

[EXO 32:25](https://ref.ly/Exod32:25) · [2CH 28:19](https://ref.ly/2Chr28:19)

Non\-Engage

to refrain literally: to break loose (from an event); hence: \= action by which humans or deities 
intentionally do not engage in a certain activity

[PRO 4:15](https://ref.ly/Prov4:15) · [EZK 24:14](https://ref.ly/Ezek24:14)

Non\-Engage

to distract literally: to cause to break loose (from an event); hence: \= causative action by which humans cause other humans to intentionally not engage in a certain activity

[EXO 5:4](https://ref.ly/Exod5:4)

Unwilling

to ignore, to neglect, to spurn literally: to break loose (from an activity); hence: \= state in which humans are unwilling to engage with a certain matter

[PRO 1:25](https://ref.ly/Prov1:25) · [PRO 8:33](https://ref.ly/Prov8:33) · [PRO 13:18](https://ref.ly/Prov13:18) · [PRO 15:32](https://ref.ly/Prov15:32)

1 JDG 5:2 MT פְּרֹעַ פְּרָעֹות NJPS "locks go untrimmed" NRSV "locks are long" NJB "unbound their hair" \| RSV ESV "leaders took the lead" NIV "princes take the lead" REB "leaders, leaders"

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Leviticus 10:6; Leviticus 13:45; Leviticus 21:10; Numbers 5:18; Judges 5:2; Exodus 32:25; Proverbs 29:18; 2 Chronicles 28:19; Proverbs 4:15; Ezekiel 24:14; Exodus 5:4; Proverbs 1:25; Proverbs 8:33; Proverbs 13:18; Proverbs 15:32


## פֶּרַע (id: 006029000000000)

פֶּרַע
======

פֶּרַע (H6545 · H6546)

noun m · פרע

People

locks \= loose hair on one's head

[NUM 6:5](https://ref.ly/Num6:5) · [DEU 32:42](https://ref.ly/Deut32:42)1 · [JDG 5:2](https://ref.ly/Judg5:2)2 · [EZK 44:20](https://ref.ly/Ezek44:20)

1 DEU 32:42 MT רֹאשׁ פַּרְעֹות RSV ESV long\-haired heads NJB "dishevelled heads" NRSV "long\-haired" \| NJPS "long\-haired chiefs" \| NIV "heads of leaders" REB "heads of princes" CEV "heads of leaders" 2 JDG 5:2 MT פְּרֹעַ פְּרָעֹות NJPS "locks go untrimmed" NRSV "locks are long" NJB "unbound their hair" \| RSV ESV "leaders took the lead" NIV "princes take the lead" REB "leaders, leaders"

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Numbers 6:5; Deuteronomy 32:42; Judges 5:2; Ezekiel 44:20

## פַּרְעֹשׁ (id: 006031000000000)

פַּרְעֹשׁ
=========

פַּרְעֹשׁ (H6550 · H6551)

noun m

Swarming Creatures

Scatter

to scatter, to spread literally: to cause to spread out; hence: \= causative action by which deities cause humans or objects to divide themselves and move into many different directions

## פֵּשֶׁת (id: 006067000000000)

פֵּשֶׁת
=======

פֵּשֶׁת (H6593 · H6594) — פִּשְׁתָּה [SAHD](https://sahd-online.com/words/pishthah/)

noun c

Crops

flax \= product of a plant of about a meter tall; its leaves are narrow and the flowers are bright blue with five petals; ► the seed capsule contains oil; after the plants have ripened they are uprooted and the stalks are left to dry for a while; they are then soaked, dried, and beaten to separate the fibers, which are then combed and woven into linen cloth

[EXO 9:31](https://ref.ly/Exod9:31) · [EXO 9:31](https://ref.ly/Exod9:31) · [JOS 2:6](https://ref.ly/Josh2:6) · [JDG 15:14](https://ref.ly/Judg15:14) · [PRO 31:13](https://ref.ly/Prov31:13) · [ISA 19:9](https://ref.ly/Isa19:9) · [HOS 2:7](https://ref.ly/Hos2:7) · [HOS 2:11](https://ref.ly/Hos2:11)

Professions

**Collocation:** עֹבְדֵי פִּשְׁתִּים שְׂרִיקֹות

workers in combed flax \= people whose profession it is to clean flax by combing it

[ISA 19:9](https://ref.ly/Isa19:9)

Cloth

linen \= woven material made from the stems of the flax plant; absorbs perspiration better than many other types of cloth; ► used for production of cloth and clothes, but can also be used as a measuring line; worn by priests; ≈ associated with quality, strength, and coolness

[LEV 13:47](https://ref.ly/Lev13:47) · [LEV 13:48](https://ref.ly/Lev13:48) · [LEV 13:52](https://ref.ly/Lev13:52) · [LEV 13:59](https://ref.ly/Lev13:59) · [DEU 22:11](https://ref.ly/Deut22:11) · [JER 13:1](https://ref.ly/Jer13:1) · [EZK 40:3](https://ref.ly/Ezek40:3) · [EZK 44:17](https://ref.ly/Ezek44:17) · [EZK 44:18](https://ref.ly/Ezek44:18) · [EZK 44:18](https://ref.ly/Ezek44:18)

Furnishings

wick \= a strip of cotton that, when placed in a lamp, draws up the oil on one side and is set alight on the other

[ISA 42:3](https://ref.ly/Isa42:3) · [ISA 43:17](https://ref.ly/Isa43:17)

Reinier de Blois

## פתה (id: 006073000000000)

פתה
===

verb · פֶּתִי · פְּתַיּוּת

## פתל (id: 006089000000000)

פתל
===

פתל (H6617)

verb · נַפְתּוּלִים · פָּתִיל · נַפְתָּלִי

Conflict

**Collocation:** פתל נַפְתּוּלִים

to struggle, to fight literally: to wrestle; hence: \= action by which humans are in a fierce competition with other humans and make a huge effort to prevail over the other

[GEN 30:8](https://ref.ly/Gen30:8)1

verb · פְּתַלְתֹּל

Evil

wily, cunning, deceitful \= state in which humans are intent on outwitting, tricking, or deceiving other humans

[JOB 5:13](https://ref.ly/Job5:13)

Evil

to treat (someone) according to (his own) crookedness \= action by which deities act like humans that are intent on outwitting, tricking, and deceiving other humans

[2SA 22:27](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:27)2 · [PSA 18:27](https://ref.ly/Ps18:27)

Unfaithful

**Collocation:** פתל

false, deceitful, misleading \= process of being done with the intention to outwit, trick, or deceive other people; ≈ can have both a positive and a negative sense

[PRO 8:8](https://ref.ly/Prov8:8)

1 GEN 30:8 RSV NIV NJPS NJB NRSV GNT CEV \= \[1] \| REB "I have devised a fine trick against my sister" \= \[2] 2 2SA 22:27 MT תִּתָּפָּל \= תפל

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Genesis 30:8; Job 5:13; 2 Samuel 22:27; Psalms 18:27; Proverbs 8:8

## פֶּתֶן (id: 006092000000000)

פֶּתֶן
======

פֶּתֶן (H6620)

noun m · מִפְתָּן

Small Animals

asp, cobra \= snake with the ability to spread the ribs in the neck area, so as to form a broad, flat profile called the hood, which makes it look thicker than it really is; reaches two meters in length and 50 millimeters in diameter; it is dark brown with a yellowish underside; very poisonous; feeds on mice, gerbils, birds, bird eggs, lizards, frogs, and other snakes; ≈ associated with great danger

[DEU 32:33](https://ref.ly/Deut32:33) · [JOB 20:14](https://ref.ly/Job20:14) · [JOB 20:16](https://ref.ly/Job20:16) · [PSA 58:5](https://ref.ly/Ps58:5) · [PSA 91:13](https://ref.ly/Ps91:13) · [ISA 11:8](https://ref.ly/Isa11:8)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Deuteronomy 32:33; Job 20:14; Job 20:16; Psalms 58:5; Psalms 91:13; Isaiah 11:8
